<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>label_added</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>label</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique Identifier of a Label.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>label_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Label title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>reason</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Reason for label addition, removal, or value change event. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>copy</code><br>Reason for change Drive item copy.</li><li><code>default_label</code><br>Reason for change default label behavior.</li><li><code>dlp_action</code><br>Reason for change DLP.</li><li><code>reason_unspecified</code><br>Reason for change unspecified.</li><li><code>user_action</code><br>Reason for change is a user action.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>label_added</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> applied Label <var>{label_title}</var>.</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Label applied on creation

Label was applied automatically when the Drive item was created.

### Label removed

Label was removed.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>label_removed</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. ### Lock

Document lock.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>add_lock</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>lock_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The lock type on an item. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>domain_admin</code><br>Domain Admin lock type.</li><li><code>editor</code><br>Editor lock type.</li><li><code>owner</code><br>Owner lock type.</li><li><code>unknown_lock_type</code><br>Unknown lock type.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>add_lock</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> locked an item</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>source_folder_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Source folder Id.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>source_folder_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Source folder title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>remove_from_folder</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> removed an item from <var>{source_folder_title}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Rename

Document rename.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>rename</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>new_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>New Value.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Value.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>rename</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> renamed <var>{old_value}</var> to <var>{new_value}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>pin_revision</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>revision_create_timestamp</code></td><td><p><code>integer</code></p><p>The timestamp when the revision was originally created (in epoch microseconds).</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>revision_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The ID of the revision.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>pin_revision</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> pinned a revision of this item</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Revision unpinned

A revision of an item was unpinned, indicating that the revision should not be kept forever.

See the <a href="https://developers.google.com/apps-script/guides/bound">Container-bound Scripts documentation</a> for more information about container applications. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Google Docs application.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Google Forms application.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Google Sites application.</li><li><code>slides</code><br>Google Slides application.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Google Sheets application.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown application.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>script_container_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The container ID of a container-bound Apps Script file. See the <a href="https://developers.google.com/apps-script/guides/triggers/installable">Apps Script Installable Triggers documentation</a> for more information about script triggers. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>calendar</code><br>Google Calendar application.</li><li><code>clock</code><br>System time.</li><li><code>document</code><br>Google Docs application.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Google Forms application.</li><li><code>slides</code><br>Google Slides application.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Google Sheets application.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown application.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>script_trigger_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Script trigger type. See the <a href="https://developers.google.com/apps-script/guides/triggers/installable">Apps Script Installable Triggers documentation</a> for more information about script triggers. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>event_any</code><br>On any event.</li><li><code>event_on_change</code><br>On change.</li><li><code>event_on_edit</code><br>On edit.</li><li><code>event_on_event_created</code><br>On calendar event created.</li><li><code>event_on_event_deleted</code><br>On calendar event deleted.</li><li><code>event_on_event_updated</code><br>On calendar event updated.</li><li><code>event_on_form_submit</code><br>On form submit.</li><li><code>event_on_open</code><br>On open.</li><li><code>timed_oneshot</code><br>Oneshot.</li><li><code>timed_recurring</code><br>Recurring.</li><li><code>trigger_type_unspecified</code><br>Trigger type unspecified.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. See the <a href="https://developers.google.com/apps-script/guides/triggers/installable">Apps Script Installable Triggers documentation</a> for more information about script triggers. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>event_any</code><br>On any event.</li><li><code>event_on_change</code><br>On change.</li><li><code>event_on_edit</code><br>On edit.</li><li><code>event_on_event_created</code><br>On calendar event created.</li><li><code>event_on_event_deleted</code><br>On calendar event deleted.</li><li><code>event_on_event_updated</code><br>On calendar event updated.</li><li><code>event_on_form_submit</code><br>On form submit.</li><li><code>event_on_open</code><br>On open.</li><li><code>timed_oneshot</code><br>Oneshot.</li><li><code>timed_recurring</code><br>Recurring.</li><li><code>trigger_type_unspecified</code><br>Trigger type unspecified.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>delete_script_trigger</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> deleted a script trigger</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Sheets Import Url

A Google Sheet fetched one or more urls via an [Import function](https://support.google.com/docs/answer/12188454).

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>sheets_import_url</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>accessed_url</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The URLs that were accessed.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>sheets_import_url</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code>A url was imported from this item</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Source Copy

Source document copy. This event is present for the original item that was copied. The `copy` event is present for the newly created item.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>source_copy</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>copy_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Indicates whether the original item and new item are owned by the same organization. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>external</code><br>The original item and new item are not owned by the same organization.</li><li><code>internal</code><br>The original item and new item are owned by the same organization.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>encryption_change</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The encryption change that happened as part of this document modification. An unset value indicates that no encryption change happened. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>decrypted_copy</code><br>An unencrypted item was created from an encrypted item.</li><li><code>encrypted_copy</code><br>An encrypted item was created from an unencrypted item.</li><li><code>encrypted_in_place</code><br>An unencrypted item was encrypted in-place.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>new_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The title of the newly created document.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The title of the original document.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>create_suggestion</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> created a suggestion</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Sync client paused

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>pause_sync_client</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>target_user</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the affected user.</p></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>pause_sync_client</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code>File syncing paused for <var>{target_user}</var> due to potential ransomware.</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>lock_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The lock type on an item. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>remove_lock</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> unlocked an item</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>track_name</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Video caption track name.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>delete_video_caption</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> deleted a video caption</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Video caption downloaded

Download video caption.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>download_video_caption</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>track_name</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Video caption track name.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>download_video_caption</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> downloaded a video caption</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>shared_drive_apply_security_update</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> applied the security update to all files in a shared drive</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>auto</code><br>Publish Live File.</li><li><code>fixed</code><br>Publish a Version.</li><li><code>none</code><br>Unpublished.</li><li><code>unchanged</code><br>Unchanged.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>publish_change</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> changed publish status from <var>{old_value}</var> to <var>{new_value}</var> and changed visibility from <var>{old_publish_visibility}</var> to <var>{new_publish_visibility}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Editor Settings Change

Editor Settings Changed.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>change_acl_editors</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>new_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>New Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>owner</code><br>The person modifying the access on the file is the Owner of the file.</li><li><code>writers</code><br>The person modifying the access on the file is a Writer (Editor) of the file.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>owner</code><br>The person modifying the access on the file is the Owner of the file.</li><li><code>writers</code><br>The person modifying the access on the file is a Writer (Editor) of the file.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Visibility of Target File. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility_change</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Change in overall visibility of the file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>external</code><br>Overall visibility changed from internal to external.</li><li><code>internal</code><br>Overall visibility changed from external to internal.</li><li><code>none</code><br>No change in overall visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>change_acl_editors</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> changed editor settings from <var>{old_value}</var> to <var>{new_value}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>target_domain</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Optional. The domain for which the access scope was changed. This can also be the alias <code>all</code> to indicate the access scope was changed for all domains that have visibility for this document.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility_change</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Change in overall visibility of the file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>external</code><br>Overall visibility changed from internal to external.</li><li><code>internal</code><br>Overall visibility changed from external to internal.</li><li><code>none</code><br>No change in overall visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>change_document_access_scope</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> changed link sharing access type from <var>{old_value}</var> to <var>{new_value}</var> for <var>{target_domain}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Link Sharing Access Type Change from Parent Folder

Change in link sharing access type of document due to hierarchy reconciliation.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>change_document_access_scope_hierarchy_reconciled</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>new_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>New Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>can_comment</code><br>Can comment.</li><li><code>can_edit</code><br>Can edit.</li><li><code>can_respond</code><br>Can respond.</li><li><code>can_view</code><br>Can view.</li><li><code>can_view_published</code><br>Can view published.</li><li><code>none</code><br>Scope none.</li><li><code>organizer</code><br>Manager.</li><li><code>owner</code><br>Is a owner.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>can_comment</code><br>Can comment.</li><li><code>can_edit</code><br>Can edit.</li><li><code>can_respond</code><br>Can respond.</li><li><code>can_view</code><br>Can view.</li><li><code>can_view_published</code><br>Can view published.</li><li><code>none</code><br>Scope none.</li><li><code>organizer</code><br>Manager.</li><li><code>owner</code><br>Is a owner.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Visibility of Target File. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>.
