### Link Sharing visibility change

Change in link sharing visibility of document.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>change_document_visibility</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>new_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>New Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link on the web can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access, apart from possible sharing with individual users/groups outside the audience.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Document link not exposed, apart from possible sharing with individual users/groups (even outside the domain).</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access, apart from possible sharing with individual users/groups outside the audience.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link on the web can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access, apart from possible sharing with individual users/groups outside the audience.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Document link not exposed, apart from possible sharing with individual users/groups (even outside the domain).</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access, apart from possible sharing with individual users/groups outside the audience.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Visibility of Target File. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. This can also be the alias <code>all</code> to indicate the access scope was changed for all domains that have visibility for this document.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility_change</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Change in overall visibility of the file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>external</code><br>Overall visibility changed from internal to external.</li><li><code>internal</code><br>Overall visibility changed from external to internal.</li><li><code>none</code><br>No change in overall visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>change_document_visibility_hierarchy_reconciled</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code>Due to a change in a parent folder, the link sharing visibility for <var>{target_domain}</var> changed from <var>{old_value}</var> to <var>{new_value}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

A new version of this item was published.

Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>publish_new_version</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> published a new version</code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

If the user has multiple email addresses on their Google account, their display email is used instead of the specific email that the item was shared with.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. ### Shared Drive Settings Change

For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>target</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Target User or Group.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_settings_change_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Type of change in shared drive settings. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>cross_domain_sharing</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts the ability for the contents within the shared drive to be shared outside the domain.</li><li><code>direct_acl</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts the ability to add users directly onto a file when they're not a member.</li><li><code>download</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts a user's ability to download files from the shared drive.</li><li><code>drive_fs</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts access to Google Drive for desktop.</li><li><code>file_organizer_can_share_folders</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts a file organizer's ability to share folders.</li><li><code>readers_can_download</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts a reader’s ability to download files from the shared drive.</li><li><code>writers_can_download</code><br>A shared drive settings change that restricts or unrestricts a writer’s ability to download files from the shared drive.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>shared_drive_settings_change</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> changed <var>{shared_drive_settings_change_type}</var> setting from <var>{old_settings_state}</var> to <var>{new_settings_state}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### Sheets ImportRange access change

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>sheets_import_range_access_change</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>sheets_import_range_enabled</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the recipient Sheet is enabled to import data from this Sheet.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>sheets_import_range_recipient_doc</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Sheets ImportRange recipient doc.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>sheets_import_range_access_change</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> enabled Sheets range import to <var>{sheets_import_range_recipient_doc}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### User Sharing Permissions Change

User Sharing Permissions Changed.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>change_user_access</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>actor_is_collaborator_account</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the actor is a collaborator account.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>billable</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this activity is billable.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document ID.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_title</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>doc_type</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Document type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>document</code><br>Doc type document.</li><li><code>drawing</code><br>Doc type drawing.</li><li><code>folder</code><br>Doc type folder.</li><li><code>form</code><br>Doc type form.</li><li><code>html</code><br>Doc type HTML.</li><li><code>jam</code><br>Doc type Jam.</li><li><code>jpeg</code><br>Doc type JPEG.</li><li><code>mp4</code><br>Doc type MP4.</li><li><code>mpeg</code><br>Doc type MPEG.</li><li><code>msexcel</code><br>Doc type MS Excel.</li><li><code>mspowerpoint</code><br>Doc type MS Powerpoint.</li><li><code>msword</code><br>Doc type MS Word.</li><li><code>pdf</code><br>Doc type PDF.</li><li><code>png</code><br>Doc type PNG.</li><li><code>presentation</code><br>Doc type presentation.</li><li><code>quicktime</code><br>Doc type Quicktime.</li><li><code>script</code><br>Google Apps Script.</li><li><code>shortcut</code><br>Doc type is Google Shortcut.</li><li><code>sites</code><br>Doc type is Google Sites.</li><li><code>spreadsheet</code><br>Doc type spreadsheet.</li><li><code>shared_drive</code><br>Doc type is a shared drive.</li><li><code>txt</code><br>Doc type txt.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Doc type unknown.</li><li><code>video</code><br>Doc type is a Google Vids Video.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>is_encrypted</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether the file is client-side encrypted.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>new_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>New Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>can_comment</code><br>Can comment.</li><li><code>can_edit</code><br>Can edit.</li><li><code>can_respond</code><br>Can respond.</li><li><code>can_view</code><br>Can view.</li><li><code>can_view_published</code><br>Can view published.</li><li><code>none</code><br>Scope none.</li><li><code>organizer</code><br>Manager.</li><li><code>owner</code><br>Is a owner.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_value</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Value. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>can_comment</code><br>Can comment.</li><li><code>can_edit</code><br>Can edit.</li><li><code>can_respond</code><br>Can respond.</li><li><code>can_view</code><br>Can view.</li><li><code>can_view_published</code><br>Can view published.</li><li><code>none</code><br>Scope none.</li><li><code>organizer</code><br>Manager.</li><li><code>owner</code><br>Is a owner.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>old_visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Old Visibility of Target File. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>originating_app_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The Google Cloud project number of the application that performed the action. Use the <a href="https://developers.google.com/drive/v2/reference/apps/get">Drive REST API</a> to retrieve the app title.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the document's owner. For items contained in a shared drive, the owner is the name of the shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_is_shared_drive</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Boolean flag denoting whether the owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>owner_shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The shared drive root ID if the document owner is a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>primary_event</code></td><td><p><code>boolean</code></p><p>Whether this event is a primary event. A single user action in Drive can generate several events, multiple of which can be primary (<code>primary_event=true</code>). The remaining events are deemed to be side effects of the primary event(s) (<code>primary_event=false</code>). For example, when a user creates a document, several events are generated, with only the create event having <code>primary_event=true</code>. But when a user shares a document with multiple other users in one action, an access change event having <code>primary_event=true</code> is created for each sharee. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>false</code><br>Boolean value false.</li><li><code>true</code><br>Boolean value true.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>target_user</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The email address of the user or group whose access permissions were changed, or the name of the domain for which access permissions were changed. If the user has multiple email addresses on their Google account, their display email is used instead of the specific email that the item was shared with.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>shared_drive_id</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>The unique identifier of the shared drive. Only populated for events or items from a shared drive.</p></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Visibility of target file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>people_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link can access.</li><li><code>people_within_domain_with_link</code><br>Anyone with the link within the audience can access.</li><li><code>private</code><br>Private.</li><li><code>public_in_the_domain</code><br>Anyone within the audience can access.</li><li><code>public_on_the_web</code><br>Public on the web.</li><li><code>shared_externally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups external to the domain.</li><li><code>shared_internally</code><br>Shared with explicit users/groups internal to the domain.</li><li><code>unknown</code><br>Unknown visibility.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><code>visibility_change</code></td><td><p><code>string</code></p><p>Change in overall visibility of the file. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>external</code><br>Overall visibility changed from internal to external.</li><li><code>internal</code><br>Overall visibility changed from external to internal.</li><li><code>none</code><br>No change in overall visibility.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>change_user_access</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code><var>{actor}</var> changed sharing permissions for <var>{target_user}</var> from <var>{old_value}</var> to <var>{new_value}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

## Pooled quota metadata

Events of this type are returned with `type=pooled_quota_metadata`.

### Storage Usage Update

Drive storage usage update.

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2">Event details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Event name</td><td><code>storage_usage_update</code></td></tr><tr><td>Parameters</td><td><table><tbody><tr><td><code>storage_usage_in_bytes</code></td><td><p><code>integer</code></p><p>Storage usage (in bytes).</p></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><td>Sample request</td><td><div><code>GET https://admin.googleapis.com/admin/reports/v1/activity/users/all/applications/<b>drive</b>?eventName=<b>storage_usage_update</b>&maxResults=10&access_token=<var>YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN</var></code></div></td></tr><tr><td>Admin Console message format</td><td><div><code>Storage usage update for <var>{actor}</var></code></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
